# Part 2: RAWGraphs (1)

A different way to see the evolution in time of the General Government Debt per country by using a Beeswarm plot. The data here shows the evolution of debt per country from 1995 to 2018.

# Part 3: RAWGraphs (2)

Trying to improve the previous way of presenting the information experimenting with different types of charts. Initially I tried with Circle Packing, but it makes difficut to understand the evolution of data year by year. Also, it is not easy to identify the name of the country in each cluster of circles. I decided to change my approach and started using charts that allowed me to represent a time series. My first attempt was with the Horizon Graph. Color cannot be changed by country, and the information is more "packed". Differences per year are not very notorious, but is a good first approach.

I decided to keep the same idea, with the same color for each country but this time I wanted to make the differences more notorious to the audience. I chose to use an Area Graph, unified all colors to gray, because we are talking about the same variable in the data (value of debt) and finally painted COL with red to keep the uniformity with the original OECD graph. I used cardinal interpolation to get smoother transitions within the data and sorted by total (ascending). The following are the achieved results:

# Circle Packing
